name:Z‚Äçh‚Äçi‚Äçj‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçz‚Äçh‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçe

posted:Posted May 16, 2024
msg:I was fortunate to stay in this hotel and had a great time here. I would like to share my experience and make an objective evaluation of all aspects of the hotel.
1. The geographical location is relatively superior, 18 minutes walk from the ancient city wall of Datong, and it is also close to Huayan Temple, Shanhua Ancient Temple, Nine Dragon Wall and other places, and it only takes a few minutes by taxi.
2. The hotel has a beautiful and comfortable environment, complete facilities, and a friendly and enthusiastic service attitude, making guests feel at home.
3. The guest rooms are clean and tidy, the bathroom is separated into dry and wet areas, and the spacious and humanized layout is reasonable.
4. The hotel's breakfast is rich and delicious. Not only does it provide local specialties, such as knife-cut noodles, but also a variety of fresh Western dishes, so that guests can enjoy it to their heart's content.
5. After staying for two nights, fresh fruit plates and snacks were delivered every morning. Such thoughtful and meticulous service made me feel the warmth of home, which also reflects the hotel's respect and care for guests, and also shows the hotel's spirit of pursuing excellent service quality.
However, in terms of room facilities, I found some areas that can be improved. First of all, there is no USB socket in the room, which does bring some inconvenience to modern travelers because we often need to use various electronic devices. Secondly, although the Kohler toilet looks beautiful, it is not very comfortable to sit on. In addition, the flap has no shock absorption function and is noisy when used, which may affect other guests' rest. I hope the hotel can consider these feedbacks and upgrade and improve the facilities accordingly so that future guests can have a more comfortable and convenient stay experience.
Overall, I was deeply impressed by this hotel. Whether it is service, facilities or environment, it shows high quality and professionalism. I strongly recommend this hotel to all travelers who seek comfort and convenience. Looking forward to the next stay!
